@@117881934 @6881934/ <h> How the VAT free scheme works : <p> If you are a registered wheelchair user in the UK , then Orangewheels may be able to help you in your next new car purchase , by not only offering you a big discount on the car , but also selling the car VAT free . Please be aware this is not part of the Motability scheme , this is an entirely separate zero-rate VAT arrangement through HM revenue and customs for customers who are purchasing brand new vehicles outright , not using finance . <p> You can purchase a new car VAT free in the UK if you meet ALL of the following criteria : <p> The car is purchased by a disabled person who normally uses a wheelchair to be get around . <p> The vehicle is permanently and substantially adapted for the purpose , e.g. the fitment of hand controls . ( more below ) <p> The vehicle is for personal use only of the disabled wheelchair user <p> The selling dealership is provided with a completed form VAT1615A declaration to confirm the users eligibility . <p> @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ and temporary use of a wheelchair e.g. for shopping trips or due to an injury like a broken leg also does not qualify . <p> Adaptations to the vehicle must be permanent and substantial , and specific to the users requirements , allowing the user to enter , exit or drive the vehicle when it would not otherwise be possible . Examples include : <p> A swivelling seat <p> A hoist to lift the user into the vehicle <p> Push-Pull brake &amp; accelerator hand controls <p> A wheelchair box fitted to the back of the vehicle <p> Minor adaptations such as steering knobs do not qualify , or options such as automatic gearboxes , parking sensors , a roofrack or trailer do not qualify as they are general adaptations and not specifically designed for wheelchair use . <p> Because there have been a well known number of abuses of this scheme where users have been purchasing multiple new cars and selling them on at a profit , and HMRC has taken the user to court and prosecuted them , dealers are now rightly cautious about misuse of the VAT free @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ @ uses will run a background check on any potential purchaser to see if they have bought a car using this scheme in the last 12 months - if they have done so , both Orangewheels and our supplying dealerships will decline the sale . <p> All of the prices shown on our website will include VAT ( and sometimes finance offers too ) , so if you submit an enquiry via the website , we can contact you and confirm the final VAT free sale price . <p> For further information and for the relevant declaration form , follow this link to the HMRC website : HMRC VAT1615 Helpsheet.
